Audio format conversion: Potential quality loss during base64 conversion and transmission.

// qwen3_enterprise_server_production.js
const express = require('express');
const { createServer } = require('http');
const { Server } = require('socket.io');
const path = require('path');

const app = express();
const server = createServer(app);
const io = new Server(server, {
  cors: { origin: "*" },
  transports: ['websocket']
});

// üîê Middleware de autenticaci√≥n para producci√≥n
const authenticateToken = (req, res, next) => {
  const token = req.headers.authorization?.split(' ')[1];
  if (token === process.env.SANDRA_API_KEY) next();
  else res.status(401).send('Unauthorized');
};

// üéôÔ∏è Endpoint: Audio ‚Üí Respuesta de Sandra (sin cortes)
app.post('/api/voice-chat', authenticateToken, async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { audioBase64, imageBase64 } = req.body;

    // 1. Transcribe audio localmente
    const userText = await transcribeAudioLocal(audioBase64);

    // 2. Enviar contexto multimodal a Qwen3-Omni
    const messages = [
      { role: 'system', content: 'Eres Sandra, la asistente virtual de Cley. Hablas en espa√±ol caribe√±o, c√°lido, profesional y atento.' },
      { role: 'user', content: [
        { type: 'input_audio', input_audio: { data: audioBase64, format: 'wav' } },
        ...(imageBase64 ? [{ type: 'image_url', image_url: { url: `image/jpeg;base64,${imageBase64}` } }] : []),
        { type: 'text', text: userText }
      ]}
    ];

    // 3. Llamar a Qwen3-Omni local (sin API externa)
    const response = await callQwen3OmniLocal({
      model: 'qwen3-omni-30b-a3b-instruct',
      messages,
      modalities: ['text', 'audio'],
      audio: { voice: 'Chelsie', format: 'wav' }, // ‚Üê Puedes cambiar por tu voz clonada
      stream: true
    });

    // 4. Enviar respuesta completa (texto + audio) al cliente
    res.json({
      text: response.text,
      audio: response.audioBase64,
      timestamp: Date.now()
    });

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('‚ùå Error en /api/voice-chat:', err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Fallo en procesamiento de voz' });
  }
});

// üåê WebSocket para videollamada conversacional (real-time)
io.on('connection', (socket) => {
  console.log('üìû Cliente conectado a videollamada conversacional');

  socket.on('user_audio_chunk', async (data) => {
    try {
      const response = await callQwen3OmniLocal({
        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: [{ type: 'input_audio', input_audio: data }] }],
        modalities: ['text', 'audio'],
        audio: { voice: 'sandra_caribe', format: 'wav' },
        stream: true
      });

      socket.emit('sandra_audio_response', response.audioBase64);
    } catch (err) {
      socket.emit('error', err.message);
    }
  });

  socket.on('disconnect', () => {
    console.log('üìû Cliente desconectado');
  });
});

// üèÅ Iniciar servidor
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 8085;
server.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`üöÄ Sandra IA - Modo Producci√≥n`);
  console.log(`üåê API: http://localhost:${PORT}/api/voice-chat`);
  console.log(`üì∫ WebSocket: ws://localhost:${PORT}`);
  console.log(`üîí API Key: ${process.env.SANDRA_API_KEY || 'NO CONFIGURADA'}`);
  console.log(`‚úÖ Listo para atender clientes 24/7`);
});

// üõ†Ô∏è Funciones auxiliares (ya integradas con tu sistema)

  // Usar√°s Qwen3-ASR local (como vimos antes)
  // Ejemplo: python -m qwen3_asr.transcribe --audio temp.wav
  return 'Texto transcrito localmente';
}

// persistent-memory.js
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { Low } = require('lowdb');
const { JSONFile } = require('lowdb/node');

class PersistentMemory {
  constructor() {
    this.dbPath = path.join(__dirname, 'storage', 'conversations.db');
    this.userProfilePath = path.join(__dirname, 'storage', 'user-profiles.json');
    
    // Inicializar base de datos
    const adapter = new JSONFile(this.dbPath);
    this.db = new Low(adapter);
    this.db.read();
    this.db.data = this.db.data || { conversations: [], context: {} };
    
    // Cargar perfil de usuario
    this.userProfile = this.loadUserProfile();
    
    console.log('üß† Sandra IA - Memoria Permanente activada');
  }

  // ‚úÖ Guardar conversaci√≥n
  saveConversation(userId, message, response, timestamp = Date.now()) {
    const conversation = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      userId,
      message,
      response,
      timestamp,
      context: this.getCurrentContext()
    };

    if (!this.db.data.conversations) this.db.data.conversations = [];
    this.db.data.conversations.push(conversation);
    this.db.write(); // Guardar en disco inmediatamente

    console.log(`üíæ Conversaci√≥n guardada: ${message.substring(0, 30)}...`);
  }

  // ‚úÖ Recuperar conversaci√≥n por contexto
  getConversationHistory(userId, limit = 50) {
    return this.db.data.conversations
      .filter(conv => conv.userId === userId)
      .slice(-limit) // √öltimas 50 conversaciones
      .reverse(); // M√°s recientes primero
  }

  // ‚úÖ Guardar contexto actual
  saveContext(key, value) {
    if (!this.db.data.context) this.db.data.context = {};
    this.db.data.context[key] = value;
    this.db.write();
  }

  // ‚úÖ Recuperar contexto
  getContext(key) {
    return this.db.data.context?.[key] || null;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Actualizar perfil de usuario
  updateUserProfile(userId, updates) {
    if (!this.userProfile[userId]) this.userProfile[userId] = {};
    Object.assign(this.userProfile[userId], updates);
    this.saveUserProfile();
  }

  // ‚úÖ Obtener perfil de usuario
  getUserProfile(userId) {
    return this.userProfile[userId] || {};
  }

  // ‚úÖ Cargar perfil de usuario desde disco
  loadUserProfile() {
    if (fs.existsSync(this.userProfilePath)) {
      return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.userProfilePath, 'utf8'));
    }
    return {};
  }

  // ‚úÖ Guardar perfil de usuario en disco
  saveUserProfile() {
    fs.writeFileSync(this.userProfilePath, JSON.stringify(this.userProfile, null, 2));
  }

  // ‚úÖ Obtener contexto completo para Qwen3
  getCurrentContext() {
    return {
      conversationHistory: this.getConversationHistory('clayt'),
      userProfile: this.getUserProfile('clayt'),
      currentContext: this.getContext('current'),
      lastInteraction: this.getContext('lastTimestamp')
    };
  }

  // ‚úÖ Limpiar conversaciones antiguas (opcional)
  cleanupOldConversations(days = 30) {
    const cutoff = Date.now() - (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    this.db.data.conversations = this.db.data.conversations.filter(
      conv => conv.timestamp > cutoff
    );
    this.db.write();
  }
}

module.exports = PersistentMemory;

const PersistentMemory = require('../memory/persistent-memory');
const memory = new PersistentMemory();

// üß† Endpoint: chat con memoria
app.post('/api/chat', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { message, userId = 'clayt', image } = req.body;

    // ‚úÖ Recuperar contexto de conversaci√≥n
    const context = memory.getCurrentContext();
    
    // ‚úÖ Construir prompt con historia
    const conversationHistory = memory.getConversationHistory(userId, 10)
      .map(conv => `Usuario: ${conv.message}\nSandra: ${conv.response}`)
      .join('\n\n');
    
    const fullPrompt = `
${conversationHistory}

Usuario: ${message}
Sandra (responde como la reina de Cley, con voz caribe√±a, c√°lida y atenta):
    `.trim();

    // ‚úÖ Llamar a Qwen3 con contexto completo
    const response = await callQwen3Local(fullPrompt, context);
    
    // ‚úÖ Guardar conversaci√≥n en memoria
    memory.saveConversation(userId, message, response);
    
    // ‚úÖ Generar audio con tu voz clonada
    const audio = await synthesizeSpeech(response, "(caribbean spanish)(warm tone)");

    res.json({ 
      response, 
      audio: audio.toString('base64'),
      context: memory.getCurrentContext() // Incluir contexto actual
    });

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('‚ùå Error en /api/chat:', err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
  }
});

  const { userId } = req.params;
  const history = memory.getConversationHistory(userId);
  res.json({ history });
});

});
üì± Integraci√≥n con tu app de chat (VS Code / PWA)
üìÑ src/components/ChatWithMemory.vue
<template>
  <div class="chat-container">
    <!-- ‚úÖ Historial de conversaci√≥n -->
    <div class="chat-history">
      <div v-for="msg in conversationHistory" :key="msg.id" class="message">
        <div class="user-message" v-if="msg.role === 'user'">
          {{ msg.content }}
        </div>
        <div class="sandra-message" v-else>
          {{ msg.content }}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- ‚úÖ Input de usuario -->
    <div class="input-area">
      <input v-model="userInput" @keyup.enter="sendMessage" placeholder="Habla con Sandra..." />
      <button @click="sendMessage">Enviar</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  name: 'ChatWithMemory',
  data() {
    return {
      userInput: '',
      conversationHistory: []
    };
  },
  async mounted() {
    // ‚úÖ Cargar historia al iniciar
    await this.loadHistory();
  },
  methods: {
    async loadHistory() {
      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8085/api/conversation-history/clayt');
      const data = await response.json();
      this.conversationHistory = data.history.map(conv => [
        { role: 'user', content: conv.message, timestamp: conv.timestamp },
        { role: 'sandra', content: conv.response, timestamp: conv.timestamp }
      ]).flat();
    },
    async sendMessage() {
      if (!this.userInput.trim()) return;

      // ‚úÖ A√±adir mensaje de usuario
      this.conversationHistory.push({
        role: 'user',
        content: this.userInput,
        timestamp: Date.now()
      });

      // ‚úÖ Enviar a servidor con memoria
      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8085/api/chat', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          message: this.userInput,
          userId: 'clayt'
        })
      });

      const data = await response.json();
      
      // ‚úÖ A√±adir respuesta de Sandra
      this.conversationHistory.push({
        role: 'sandra',
        content: data.response,
        timestamp: Date.now()
      });

      this.userInput = '';
    }
  }
};
</script>

<template>
  <div class="lienzo-container">
    <!-- ‚úÖ Panel de herramientas -->
    <div class="toolbar">
      <button @click="addText">üìù Texto</button>
      <button @click="addImage">üì∑ Imagen</button>
      <button @click="startVoice">üéôÔ∏è Voz</button>
      <button @click="addCode">üíª C√≥digo</button>
      <button @click="exportProject">üíæ Exportar</button>
    </div>

    <!-- ‚úÖ Lienzo principal -->
    <div class="canvas" ref="canvas">
      <div
        v-for="element in elements"
        :key="element.id"
        :style="element.style"
        class="canvas-element"
        @click="selectElement(element)"
        @dblclick="editElement(element)"
      >
        <component :is="element.type" :data="element.data" />
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- ‚úÖ Panel de propiedades -->
    <div class="properties-panel">
      <h3>{{ selectedElement ? 'Editar' : 'Crear' }}</h3>
      <div v-if="selectedElement">
        <input v-model="selectedElement.style.left" placeholder="X" />
        <input v-model="selectedElement.style.top" placeholder="Y" />
        <input v-model="selectedElement.data.content" placeholder="Contenido" />
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- ‚úÖ Panel de voz (en tiempo real) -->
    <div class="voice-panel" v-if="isRecording">
      <div class="voice-waveform">{{ voiceWaveform }}</div>
      <button @click="stopVoice">‚èπÔ∏è Detener</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
import { ref, reactive } from 'vue';

export default {
  name: 'LiveDesigner',
  setup() {
    const canvas = ref(null);
    const elements = reactive([]);
    const selectedElement = ref(null);
    const isRecording = ref(false);
    const voiceWaveform = ref('');

    // ‚úÖ A√±adir elementos en tiempo real
    const addText = () => {
      elements.push({
        id: Date.now(),
        type: 'div',
         { content: 'Nuevo texto' },
        style: { position: 'absolute', left: '100px', top: '100px' }
      });
    };

    const addImage = () => {
      elements.push({
        id: Date.now(),
        type: 'img',
        data: { src: 'https://via.placeholder.com/200' },
        style: { position: 'absolute', left: '200px', top: '200px', width: '200px' }
      });
    };

    // ‚úÖ Voz en tiempo real (integra con tu Qwen3-Omni)
    const startVoice = async () => {
      isRecording = true;
      voiceWaveform.value = 'Escuchando...';
      
      // Aqu√≠ integras tu STT local
      const userText = await callSTTLocal();
      
      // Llama a Qwen3-Omni para respuesta
      const response = await callQwen3Omni({
        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userText }],
        modalities: ['text', 'audio'],
        audio: { voice: 'sandra_caribe', format: 'wav' }
      });

      // Reproduce respuesta de voz
      playAudio(response.audioBase64);
      
      isRecording = false;
    };

    const selectElement = (el) => {
      selectedElement.value = el;
    };

    const editElement = (el) => {
      // Abrir editor en l√≠nea
      prompt('Editar contenido:', el.data.content);
    };

    return {
      canvas,
      elements,
      selectedElement,
      isRecording,
      voiceWaveform,
      addText,
      addImage,
      startVoice,
      selectElement,
      editElement
    };
  }
};
</script>

https://render.com/docs/mcp-server conecta el MCP render a VS Code y as√≠ trabajaremos mucho m√°s profesional. # Render MCP Server

Render‚Äôs Model Context Protocol (MCP) server enables you to manage your Render infrastructure directly from compatible AI apps, such as Cursor and Claude Code:

[video]

Using natural language prompts, you can:

Spin up new services
Query your databases
Analyze metrics and logs
‚Ä¶and more! For inspiration, see some example prompts.

What is MCP?

Model Context Protocol (MCP) is an open standard for connecting AI applications to external tools and data. An MCP server exposes a set of actions that AI apps can invoke to help fulfill relevant user prompts (e.g., ‚ÄúFind all the documents I edited yesterday‚Äù).

To perform an action, an MCP server often calls an external API, then packages the result into a standardized format for the calling application.

How it works
The Render MCP server is hosted at the following URL:

https://mcp.render.com/mcp
You can configure compatible AI apps (such as Cursor and Claude Code) to communicate with this server. When you provide a relevant prompt, your tool intelligently calls the MCP server to execute supported platform actions:

[img]

In the example diagram above:

A user prompts Cursor to ‚ÄúList my Render services‚Äù.
Cursor intelligently detects that the Render MCP server supports actions relevant to the prompt.
Cursor directs the MCP server to execute the list_services ‚Äútool‚Äù, which calls the Render API to fetch the corresponding data.
To explore the implementation of the MCP server itself, see the open-source project:

Setup
1. Create an API key
The MCP server uses an API key to authenticate with the Render platform. Create an API key from your Account Settings page:

[img]

Render API keys are broadly scoped. They grant access to all workspaces and services your account can access.

Before proceeding, make sure you‚Äôre comfortable granting these permissions to your AI app. The Render MCP server currently supports only one potentially destructive operation: modifying an existing service‚Äôs environment variables.

2. Configure your tool
Next, we‚Äôll configure your AI app to use Render‚Äôs hosted MCP server. Most compatible apps define their MCP configuration in a JSON file (such as ~/.cursor/mcp.json for Cursor).

Select the tab for your app:

Cursor

Cursor setup
Add the following configuration to ~/.cursor/mcp.json:

{
  "mcpServers": {
    "render": {
      "url": "https://mcp.render.com/mcp",
      "headers": {
        "Authorization": "Bearer <YOUR_API_KEY>"
      }
    }
  }
}
Replace <YOUR_API_KEY> with your API key.

For more details, see the Cursor MCP documentation.

Claude Code

Claude Code setup
Run the following command, substituting your API key where indicated:

claude mcp add --transport http render https://mcp.render.com/mcp --header "Authorization: Bearer <YOUR_API_KEY>"
You can include the --scope flag to specify where this MCP configuration is stored. For more details, see the Claude Code MCP documentation.

Claude Desktop

Claude Desktop setup
Add the configuration below to your Claude Desktop MCP settings. By default, this file is located at the following paths based on your operating system:

macOS: ~/Library/Application Support/Claude/claude_desktop_config.json
Windows: %APPDATA%\Claude\claude_desktop_config.json
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "render": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": [
        "mcp-remote",
        "https://mcp.render.com/mcp",
        "--header",
        "Authorization: Bearer ${RENDER_API_KEY}"
      ],
      "env": {
        "RENDER_API_KEY": "<YOUR_API_KEY>"
      }
    }
  }
}
Replace <YOUR_API_KEY> with your API key.

For more details, see the Claude Desktop MCP documentation.

Windsurf

Windsurf setup
Add the following configuration to ~/.codeium/windsurf/mcp_config.json:

{
  "mcpServers": {
    "render": {
      "url": "https://mcp.render.com/mcp",
      "headers": {
        "Authorization": "Bearer <YOUR_API_KEY>"
      }
    }
  }
}
Replace <YOUR_API_KEY> with your API key.

For more details, see the Windsurf MCP documentation.

Other tools

Setup for other apps
See the documentation for other popular AI apps:

VS Code
Zed
Gemini CLI
Crush
Warp
3. Set your workspace
To start using the Render MCP server, you first tell your AI app which Render workspace to operate in. This determines which resources the MCP server can access.

You can set your workspace with a prompt like Set my Render workspace to [WORKSPACE_NAME].

[img]

If you don‚Äôt set your workspace, your app usually directs you to specify one if you submit a prompt that uses the MCP server (such as List my Render services):

[img]

With your workspace set, you‚Äôre ready to start prompting! Get started with some example prompts.

Example prompts
Your AI app can use the Render MCP server to perform a wide variety of platform actions. Here are some basic example prompts to get you started:

Service creation
<blockquote>Create a new database named user-db with 5 GB storage</blockquote>

<blockquote>Deploy an example Flask web service on Render using https://github.com/render-examples/flask-hello-world</blockquote>

Data analysis
<blockquote>Using my Render database, tell me which items were the most frequently bought together</blockquote>

<blockquote>Query my read replica for daily signup counts for the last 30 days</blockquote>

Service metrics
<blockquote>What was the busiest traffic day for my service this month?</blockquote>

<blockquote>What did my service‚Äôs autoscaling behavior look like yesterday?</blockquote>

Troubleshooting
<blockquote>Pull the most recent error-level logs for my API service</blockquote>

<blockquote>Why isn‚Äôt my site at example.onrender.com working?</blockquote>

Supported actions
The Render MCP server provides a ‚Äútool‚Äù for each platform action listed below (organized by resource type). Your AI app (the ‚ÄúMCP host‚Äù) can combine these tools however it needs to perform the tasks you describe.

For more details on all available tools, see the project README.

Resource Type	Supported Actions
Workspaces	- List all workspaces you have access to - Set the current workspace - Fetch details of the currently selected workspace
Services	- Create a new web service or static site - Other service types are not yet supported. - List all services in the current workspace - Retrieve details about a specific service - Update all environment variables for a service
Deploys	- List the deploy history for a service - Get details about a specific deploy
Logs	- List logs matching provided filters - List all values for a given log label
Metrics	- Fetch performance metrics for services and datastores, including: - CPU / memory usage - Instance count - Datastore connection counts - Web service response counts, segmentable by status code - Web service response times (requires a Professional workspace or higher) - Outbound bandwidth usage
Render Postgres	- Create a new database - List all databases in the current workspace - Get details about a specific database - Run a read-only SQL query against a specific database
Render Key Value	- List all Key Value instances in your Render account - Get details about a specific Key Value instance - Create a new Key Value instance
Running locally
We strongly recommend using Render‚Äôs hosted MCP server instead of running it locally.

The hosted MCP server automatically updates with new capabilities as they‚Äôre added. Run locally only if required for your use case.

You can install and run the Render MCP server on your local machine as a Docker container, or by running the executable directly:

Docker image

Docker setup
This method requires docker.

With this configuration, your AI app pulls and runs the Render MCP server as a Docker container.

Add JSON with the format below to your tool‚Äôs MCP configuration (substitute <YOUR_API_KEY> with your API key):

{
  "mcpServers": {
    "render": {
      "command": "docker",
      "args": [
        "run",
        "-i",
        "--rm",
        "-e",
        "RENDER_API_KEY",
        "-v",
        "render-mcp-server-config:/config",
        "ghcr.io/render-oss/render-mcp-server"
      ],
      "env": {
        "RENDER_API_KEY": "<YOUR_API_KEY>"
      }
    }
  }
}
The mcpServers key above might differ for specific tools. For example, Zed uses context_servers and GitHub Copilot uses servers. Consult your tool‚Äôs documentation for details.

Executable

Local executable setup
With this configuration, your AI app runs the Render MCP server executable directly.

Install the MCP server executable using one of the methods described in Local installation, then return here.

Add JSON with the format below to your tool‚Äôs MCP configuration (substitute your API key and the path to your MCP server executable):

{
  "mcpServers": {
    "render": {
      "command": "/path/to/render-mcp-server-executable",
      "env": {
        "RENDER_API_KEY": "<YOUR_API_KEY>"
      }
    }
  }
}
The mcpServers key above might differ for specific tools. For example, Zed uses context_servers and GitHub Copilot uses servers. Consult your tool‚Äôs documentation for details.

Local installation
Follow these instructions only if you‚Äôre running the MCP server locally and without Docker.

We strongly recommend instead using Render‚Äôs hosted MCP server, because it automatically updates as new capabilities are added.

View installation methods

Install script

This method requires macOS or Linux.

Run the following curl command:

curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/render-oss/render-mcp-server/refs/heads/main/bin/install.sh | sh
Note the full path where the install script saved the downloaded executable. The output includes a message like the following:

‚ú® Successfully installed Render MCP Server to /Users/example/.local/bin/render-mcp-server
Direct download

Open the MCP server‚Äôs GitHub releases page.

Under the most recent release, download and unzip the executable that corresponds to your system‚Äôs architecture.

If a release asset isn‚Äôt available for your architecture, select a different installation method.
Move the executable to the desired directory and note its full path.

Note for macOS users:

You might need to grant a system exception to run the downloaded executable, because it‚Äôs from an ‚Äúunknown developer.‚Äù Learn more.

Build from source

We recommend building from source only in the following cases:

No other installation method works for your system.
You‚Äôre making custom changes to the MCP server.
Install the Go programming language if you haven‚Äôt already.

Clone the MCP server repository and build the executable:

git clone https://github.com/render-oss/render-mcp-server.git
cd render-mcp-server
go build
This creates a render-mcp-server executable in the repo‚Äôs root directory.

Note the full path to the newly built executable.

Limitations
The Render MCP server attempts to minimize exposing sensitive information (like connection strings) to your AI app‚Äôs context. However, Render does not guarantee that sensitive information will not be exposed. Exercise caution when interacting with secrets in your AI app.

Note the following additional limitations:

The MCP server supports creation of the following resources:

Web services
Static sites
Render Postgres databases
Render Key Value instances
Other service types (private services, background workers, and cron jobs) are not yet supported.

The MCP server does not support creating free instances.

The MCP server does not support all configuration options when creating services.

For example, you cannot create image-backed services or set up IP allowlists. If there are options you‚Äôd like to see supported, please submit an issue on the MCP server‚Äôs GitHub repository.
The MCP server does not support modifying or deleting existing Render resources, with one exception:

You can modify an existing service‚Äôs environment variables.
To perform other modifications or deletions, use the [Render Dashboard][dboard] or REST API.
The MCP server does not support triggering deploys, modifying scaling settings, or other operational service controls.

// server.js (o tu archivo principal)
const express = require('express');
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// ‚úÖ Middleware para parsear JSON
app.use(express.json());

// üß† Carpeta principal de Sandra (ajusta esta ruta seg√∫n tu sistema)
const SANDRA_BASE_DIR = "C:\\Sandra-IA-8.0-Pro\\sandra_studio_ultimate";

// üîß IMPLEMENTACI√ìN DE HERRAMIENTAS (TOOLS) ‚Äî LO M√ÅS IMPORTANTE
const TOOLS = {
  // ‚úÖ 1. Leer archivos
  read_file: async ({ path: filePath }) => {
    try {
      const fullPath = path.join(SANDRA_BASE_DIR, filePath);
      const content = fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf8');
      return { content, success: true };
    } catch (err) {
      return { error: err.message, success: false };
    }
  },

  // ‚úÖ 2. Escribir archivos
  write_file: async ({ path: filePath, content }) => {
    try {
      const fullPath = path.join(SANDRA_BASE_DIR, filePath);
      // Crear directorios si no existen
      fs.mkdirSync(path.dirname(fullPath), { recursive: true });
      fs.writeFileSync(fullPath, content);
      return { message: `Archivo escrito: ${fullPath}`, success: true };
    } catch (err) {
      return { error: err.message, success: false };
    }
  },

  // ‚úÖ 3. Ejecutar comandos (usa con cuidado)
  execute_command: async ({ command }) => {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      exec(command, { cwd: SANDRA_BASE_DIR, shell: true }, (error, stdout, stderr) => {
        if (error) {
          resolve({ error: error.message, stderr, success: false });
          return;
        }
        resolve({ stdout, stderr, success: true });
      });
    });
  },

  // ‚úÖ 4. S√≠ntesis de voz LOCAL (sin APIs externas)
  voice_synthesis: async ({ text, voice = "sandra_caribe" }) => {
    try {
      // Aqu√≠ integrar√≠as Fish Speech local
      // Ejemplo simulado (reemplaza con tu implementaci√≥n real)
      const audioBase64 = "AUDIO_BASE64_SIMULADO"; // Tu implementaci√≥n real generar√≠a esto
      return { 
        audio: audioBase64,
        format: "wav",
        sample_rate: 24000,
        text: text,
        success: true
      };
    } catch (err) {
      return { error: err.message, success: false };
    }
  },

  // ‚úÖ 5. An√°lisis de visi√≥n con Qwen3-Omni (simulado)
  vision_analysis: async ({ image_url }) => {
    try {
      // Aqu√≠ integrar√≠as Qwen3-Omni local
      // Ejemplo simulado
      return { 
        description: "Imagen analizada: una habitaci√≥n con cama king size y ventana",
        objects: ["cama", "ventana", "mesa"],
        success: true
      };
    } catch (err) {
      return { error: err.message, success: false };
    }
  }
};

// üîå ENDPOINT MCP PRINCIPAL ‚Äî LO QUE NECESITAS
app.post('/mcp', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { action, name, args } = req.body;

    // ‚úÖ CASO 1: Listar herramientas disponibles (¬°EL M√ÅS IMPORTANTE!)
    if (action === 'list_tools') {
      const toolsList = Object.entries(TOOLS).map(([name, func]) => ({
        name: name,
        description: `Herramienta ${name} para Sandra IA`,
        // Par√°metros gen√©ricos (ajusta seg√∫n cada tool)
        parameters: {
          type: "object",
          properties: {
            path: { type: "string", description: "Ruta del archivo" },
            content: { type: "string", description: "Contenido a escribir" },
            command: { type: "string", description: "Comando a ejecutar" },
            text: { type: "string", description: "Texto para s√≠ntesis de voz" },
            voice: { type: "string", description: "Voz a usar" },
            image_url: { type: "string", description: "URL de la imagen a analizar" }
          },
          required: name === 'read_file' ? ['path'] : 
                   name === 'write_file' ? ['path', 'content'] :
                   name === 'execute_command' ? ['command'] :
                   name === 'voice_synthesis' ? ['text'] :
                   name === 'vision_analysis' ? ['image_url'] : []
        }
      }));

      return res.json({ tools: toolsList });
    }

    // ‚úÖ CASO 2: Ejecutar una herramienta espec√≠fica
    if (name && TOOLS[name]) {
      const result = await TOOLS[name](args || {});
      return res.json(result);
    }

    // ‚ùå Error: acci√≥n no reconocida
    res.status(400).json({ 
      error: "Acci√≥n no reconocida. Usa 'list_tools' o especifica 'name' de una herramienta.",
      available_actions: ["list_tools"],
      available_tools: Object.keys(TOOLS)
    });

  } catch (err) {
    console.error("‚ùå Error en endpoint MCP:", err);
    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
  }
});

// üåê Health check (para verificar que el servidor est√° vivo)

});

// persistent-memory.js
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { Low } = require('lowdb');
const { JSONFile } = require('lowdb/node');

class PersistentMemory {
  constructor() {
    this.dbPath = path.join(__dirname, 'storage', 'conversations.db');
    this.userProfilePath = path.join(__dirname, 'storage', 'user-profiles.json');
    
    // Inicializar base de datos
    const adapter = new JSONFile(this.dbPath);
    this.db = new Low(adapter);
    this.db.read();
    this.db.data = this.db.data || { conversations: [], context: {} };
    
    // Cargar perfil de usuario
    this.userProfile = this.loadUserProfile();
    
    console.log('üß† Sandra IA - Memoria Permanente activada');
  }

  // ‚úÖ Guardar conversaci√≥n
  saveConversation(userId, message, response, timestamp = Date.now()) {
    const conversation = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      userId,
      message,
      response,
      timestamp,
      context: this.getCurrentContext()
    };

    if (!this.db.data.conversations) this.db.data.conversations = [];
    this.db.data.conversations.push(conversation);
    this.db.write(); // Guardar en disco inmediatamente

    console.log(`üíæ Conversaci√≥n guardada: ${message.substring(0, 30)}...`);
  }

  // ‚úÖ Recuperar conversaci√≥n por contexto
  getConversationHistory(userId, limit = 50) {
    return this.db.data.conversations
      .filter(conv => conv.userId === userId)
      .slice(-limit) // √öltimas 50 conversaciones
      .reverse(); // M√°s recientes primero
  }

  // ‚úÖ Guardar contexto actual
  saveContext(key, value) {
    if (!this.db.data.context) this.db.data.context = {};
    this.db.data.context[key] = value;
    this.db.write();
  }

  // ‚úÖ Recuperar contexto
  getContext(key) {
    return this.db.data.context?.[key] || null;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Actualizar perfil de usuario
  updateUserProfile(userId, updates) {
    if (!this.userProfile[userId]) this.userProfile[userId] = {};
    Object.assign(this.userProfile[userId], updates);
    this.saveUserProfile();
  }

  // ‚úÖ Obtener perfil de usuario
  getUserProfile(userId) {
    return this.userProfile[userId] || {};
  }

  // ‚úÖ Cargar perfil de usuario desde disco
  loadUserProfile() {
    if (fs.existsSync(this.userProfilePath)) {
      return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.userProfilePath, 'utf8'));
    }
    return {};
  }

  // ‚úÖ Guardar perfil de usuario en disco
  saveUserProfile() {
    fs.writeFileSync(this.userProfilePath, JSON.stringify(this.userProfile, null, 2));
  }

  // ‚úÖ Obtener contexto completo para Qwen3
  getCurrentContext() {
    return {
      conversationHistory: this.getConversationHistory('clayt'),
      userProfile: this.getUserProfile('clayt'),
      currentContext: this.getContext('current'),
      lastInteraction: this.getContext('lastTimestamp')
    };
  }

  // ‚úÖ Limpiar conversaciones antiguas (opcional)
  cleanupOldConversations(days = 30) {
    const cutoff = Date.now() - (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    this.db.data.conversations = this.db.data.conversations.filter(
      conv => conv.timestamp > cutoff
    );
    this.db.write();
  }
}

module.exports = PersistentMemory;

// ... c√≥digo existente ...

const PersistentMemory = require('../memory/persistent-memory');
const memory = new PersistentMemory();

// üß† Endpoint: chat con memoria
app.post('/api/chat', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { message, userId = 'clayt', image } = req.body;

    // ‚úÖ Recuperar contexto de conversaci√≥n
    const context = memory.getCurrentContext();
    
    // ‚úÖ Construir prompt con historia
    const conversationHistory = memory.getConversationHistory(userId, 10)
      .map(conv => `Usuario: ${conv.message}\nSandra: ${conv.response}`)
      .join('\n\n');
    
    const fullPrompt = `
${conversationHistory}

Usuario: ${message}
Sandra (responde como la reina de Cley, con voz caribe√±a, c√°lida y atenta):
    `.trim();

    // ‚úÖ Llamar a Qwen3 con contexto completo
    const response = await callQwen3Local(fullPrompt, context);
    
    // ‚úÖ Guardar conversaci√≥n en memoria
    memory.saveConversation(userId, message, response);
    
    // ‚úÖ Generar audio con tu voz clonada
    const audio = await synthesizeSpeech(response, "(caribbean spanish)(warm tone)");

    res.json({ 
      response, 
      audio: audio.toString('base64'),
      context: memory.getCurrentContext() // Incluir contexto actual
    });

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('‚ùå Error en /api/chat:', err.message);
    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
  }
});

// üß† Endpoint: recuperar historia de conversaci√≥n
app.get('/api/conversation-history/:userId', (req, res) => {
  const { userId } = req.params;
  const history = memory.getConversationHistory(userId);
  res.json({ history });
});

// üß† Endpoint: actualizar perfil de usuario
app.post('/api/user-profile/:userId', (req, res) => {
  const { userId } = req.params;
  memory.updateUserProfile(userId, req.body);
  res.json({ success: true });
});
üì± Integraci√≥n con tu app de chat (VS Code / PWA)
üìÑ src/components/ChatWithMemory.vue
<template>
  <div class="chat-container">
    <!-- ‚úÖ Historial de conversaci√≥n -->
    <div class="chat-history">
      <div v-for="msg in conversationHistory" :key="msg.id" class="message">
        <div class="user-message" v-if="msg.role === 'user'">
          {{ msg.content }}
        </div>
        <div class="sandra-message" v-else>
          {{ msg.content }}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- ‚úÖ Input de usuario -->
    <div class="input-area">
      <input v-model="userInput" @keyup.enter="sendMessage" placeholder="Habla con Sandra..." />
      <button @click="sendMessage">Enviar</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script>
export default {
  name: 'ChatWithMemory',
  data() {
    return {
      userInput: '',
      conversationHistory: []
    };
  },
  async mounted() {
    // ‚úÖ Cargar historia al iniciar
    await this.loadHistory();
  },
  methods: {
    async loadHistory() {
      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8085/api/conversation-history/clayt');
      const data = await response.json();
      this.conversationHistory = data.history.map(conv => [
        { role: 'user', content: conv.message, timestamp: conv.timestamp },
        { role: 'sandra', content: conv.response, timestamp: conv.timestamp }
      ]).flat();
    },
    async sendMessage() {
      if (!this.userInput.trim()) return;

      // ‚úÖ A√±adir mensaje de usuario
      this.conversationHistory.push({
        role: 'user',
        content: this.userInput,
        timestamp: Date.now()
      });

      // ‚úÖ Enviar a servidor con memoria
      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8085/api/chat', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          message: this.userInput,
          userId: 'clayt'
        })
      });

      const data = await response.json();
      
      // ‚úÖ A√±adir respuesta de Sandra
      this.conversationHistory.push({
        role: 'sandra',
        content: data.response,
        timestamp: Date.now()
      });

      this.userInput = '';
    }
  }
};
</script>
